1687、To be <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/whoever">whoever</a> you want to be – there's no time <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/limit">limit</a>; start <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/whenever">whenever</a> you want. 1688、Sometimes I like to think that the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/pants">pants</a> got lost on <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/purpose">purpose</a> that this was their <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/final">final</a> <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/gift">gift</a> to us, <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/bringing">bringing</a> us back together, back to a place of <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/forgiveness">forgiveness</a> and love and an <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/understanding">understanding</a> that what we <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/shared">shared</a> was all the <a target="_blank" href="http://www.iciba.com/magic">magic</a> we could ever need.   有时候，我在想，牛仔裤是故意走丢的。这是它给予我们最后的礼物，让我们重新相聚在一起，重新享受彼此的宽恕和友爱。它让我们明白，对彼此的分享就是我们所拥有的一切魔力。—影片《牛仔裤的夏天2》<br/>
